<script>
$document.on('click', '[data-cr] input[type=submit]', function(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  var $form = $(this).closest('form[data-cr]');
  var email = $form.find('[name=\'mail\']').val();
  var origin = $form.find('[name=\'o\']').val();
  var url = BRAND().crAPI;
  var successMsg = $form.find('.success-message').html();
  var errorMsg = $form.find('.error-message').html();
  var ePar = _.cookie.get('b2wEPar') || '';
  var dataForm = $form.serialize() + '&amp;ePar=' + ePar;
  var isCrModal = $form.attr('data-cr') === 'modal';

  $form.find('.pure-button').addClass('is-ajaxloading');

  /* integraçao cr */
  //jscs:disable requireCamelCaseOrUpperCaseIdentifiers
  if (typeof crmWA_cadastro_rapido !== 'undefined') {
    crmWA_cadastro_rapido(email, origin);
  }
  //jscs:enable requireCamelCaseOrUpperCaseIdentifiers

  $.ajax({
    type: 'GET',
    url: url,
    data: dataForm,
    dataType: 'jsonp',
    success: function(data) {
      try {
        var msg = errorMsg;
        if (data == 4 || data == 1) {
          msg = successMsg;
        }
        if (isCrModal) {
          $form.find('.container-msg').html(msg);
        } else {
          $.magnificPopup.open({
            items: {
              src: msg,
              type: 'inline'
            },
            removalDelay: 300,
            mainClass: 'mfp-fade'
          });
        }
      } catch (e) {} finally {
        $form.find('.pure-button').removeClass('is-ajaxloading');
      }
    },
    error: function(xhr, type) {
      $form.find('.pure-button').removeClass('is-ajaxloading');
      $.magnificPopup.open({
        items: {
          src: errorMsg,
          type: 'inline'
        },
        removalDelay: 300,
        mainClass: 'mfp-fade'
      });
    }
  });
  return false;
});

$('.lnk-cr-politica').on('click', function () {
  var href = $(this).attr('href');

  window.location.href = href;
});
</script>
